}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n            setupEventListeners() {\\\\\\\\n                this.terminalInput.addEventListener(\\\\\\\\\\\'keypress\\\\\\\\\\\', (e) => {\\\\\\\\n                    if (e.key === this.handleApproval(false);\\\\\\\\n                });\\\\\\\\n            }\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n            addOutput(tag, message, confidence) {\\\\\\\\n                const line = \\\\\\\\n                const confBadge = document.createElement(\\\\\\\\\\\'span\\\\\\\\\\\');\\\\\\\\n                confBadge.className = `confidence-badge            line.appendChild(messageSpan);\\\\\\\\n                line.appendChild(confBadge);\\\\\\\\n                \\\\\\\\n                this.terminalOutput.appendChild(line);\\\\\\\\n                this.terminalOutput.scrollTop = this.terminalOutput.scrollHeight;\\\\\\\\n            }\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n            getConfidenceClass(conf) {\\\\\\\\n                if (conf >= 0.8) return     }\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n            updateMetrics() {\\\\\\\\n                this.operationCount++;\\\\\\\\n                document.getElementById(\\\\\\\\\\\'operationCount\\\\\\\\\\\').textContent this.updateMetrics();\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n                if (input.startsWith(\\\\\\\\\\\'/\\\\\\\\\\\')) {\\\\\\\\n                    this.processCommand(input);\\\\\\\\n                } else {\\\\\\\\n                    this.processNaturalLanguage(input);\\\\\\\\n                }\\\\\\\\n            }\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n            processCommand(cmd) {\\\\\\\\n                const parts \\\\\\\\\\\'/demo\\\\\\\\\\\':\\\\\\\\n                        this.runDemo(parts[1] || \\\\\\\\\\\'confidence_gating\\\\\\\\\\\');\\\\\\\\n                        break;\\\\\\\\n this.addOutput(\\\\\\\\\\\'E\\\\\\\\\\\', `Unknown command: ${command}`, 0.00);\\\\\\\\n                }\\\\\\\\n            }\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n            async processNaturalLanguage(query) {\\\\\\\\n                this.addOutput(\\\\\\\\\\\'I\\\\\\\\\\\', \\\\\\\\\\\'Consulting multi-LLM system...\\\\\\\\\\\', 0.85);\\\\\\\\n                \\\\\\\\n                await await this.sleep(400);\\\\\\\\n                this.addOutput(\\\\\\\\\\\'V\\\\\\\\\\\', \\\\\\\\\\\'Consensus achieved across agents\\\\\\\\\\\', 0.96);\\\\\\\\n                \\\\\\\\n }\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n            async runDemo(demoType) {\\\\\\\\n                this.addOutput(\\\\\\\\\\\'S\\\\\\\\\\\', `Starting demo: ${demoType}`, 1.00);\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n            async generateSpec(specType) {\\\\\\\\n                this.addOutput(\\\\\\\\\\\'S\\\\\\\\\\\', `Generating ${specType} specification...`, 0.90);\\\\\\\\n                \\\\\\\\n
